[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  AddressSanitizer detected an attempted double-free on a heap region at address [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x502000007310[0m[39m`. The first free occurs in the fuzzer’s static destructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39minvoked [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the second free occurs unconditionally in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_path_argument`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type:  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Memory safety violation – double-free.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations and Findings:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`systemctl_parse_argv`, which in turn calls `parse_path_argument`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `parse_path_argument` handles path strings by calling `path_make_absolute_cwd`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ `path_extend_internal`, which allocates or reallocates a buffer.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. After path processing, `parse_path_argument` frees its local buffer pointer.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Separately, the harness code’s static destructor also frees the same buffer, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to the second free on the same address.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. The failure is reproducible under AddressSanitizer with libFuzzer, indicating [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistent control flow and lifetime overlap.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected Code Areas for Investigation:  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/shared/parse-argument.c` – implementation of `parse_path_argument`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mespecially its memory allocation and free logic.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/basic/path-util.c` – functions `path_extend_internal` and [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd` where the buffer is allocated or grown.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/systemctl/systemctl.c` – entry to argument parsing [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`systemctl_parse_argv`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and how it delegates to `parse_path_argument`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c` – fuzzing harness, particularly its[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic destructor logic freeing memory.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReviewing these components will give a holistic understanding of the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation/free ownership model and clarify why the buffer is freed twice.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35malloca0[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m                                      \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m{[0m[39m                                              \[0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:                size_t _len_ = n;                       \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:                _new_ = [0m[1;35malloca_safe[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_len_[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;             \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mmemset[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_new_, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, _len_[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;                \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* It's not clear what alignment glibc/gcc [0m[1;35malloca[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m guarantee, hence provide a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguaranteed safe version *[0m[35m/[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m172[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35malloca_align[0m[1;39m([0m[39msize, align[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m                                       \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m173[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m{[0m[39m                                                              \[0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:                size_t _mask_ = [0m[1;39m([0m[39malign[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;                            \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:                size_t _size_ = size;                                   \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m177[0m[39m:                _ptr_ = [0m[1;35malloca_safe[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_size_ + _mask_[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;                   \[0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m179[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m180[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m181[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35malloca0_align[0m[1;39m([0m[39msize, align[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m                                      \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m182[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m{[0m[39m                                                              \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m183[0m[39m:                void *_new_;                                            \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m184[0m[39m:                size_t _xsize_ = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;                                \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m185[0m[39m:                _new_ = [0m[1;35malloca_align[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_xsize_, [0m[1;39m([0m[39malign[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;                 \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m186[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mmemset[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_new_, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, _xsize_[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;                              \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m187[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m188[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m189[0m[39m:#if HAS_FEATURE_MEMORY_SANITIZER[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:#  define [0m[1;35mmsan_unpoison[0m[1;39m([0m[39mr, s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35m__msan_unpoison[0m[1;39m([0m[39mr, s[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m191[0m[39m:#else[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:#  define [0m[1;35mmsan_unpoison[0m[1;39m([0m[39mr, s[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:#endif[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* Dummy allocator to tell the compiler that the new size of p is newsize. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation returns the[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m: * pointer as is; the only reason for its existence is as a conduit for the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m_alloc_ attribute.  This must not[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m: * be inlined [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhence a non-static function with _noinline_ because LTO [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39motherwise tries to inline it[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m because[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m: * gcc then loses the attributes on the function.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m: * See: [0m[4;94mhttps://gcc.gnu.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?[0m[4;94mid[0m[4;94m=[0m[4;94m96503[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:void *[0m[1;35mexpand_to_usable[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *p, size_t newsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35m_alloc_[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m _returns_nonnull_ [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m_noinline_;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/basic/alloc-util.h:[0m[1;36m104[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m110[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:static inline void [0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m106[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid**[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m107[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m108[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:#define _cleanup_free_ [0m[1;35m_cleanup_[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfreep[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/basic/alloc-util.h:[0m[1;36m104[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m110[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:static inline void [0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m106[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid**[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m107[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m108[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:#define _cleanup_free_ [0m[1;35m_cleanup_[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfreep[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify the root cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The double-free occurs because the fuzz harness invokes `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter each test, which in turn calls the `freep` cleanup function on global [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `arg_root`, `arg_image`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. However, `freep` only calls `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe pointer without nulling it. On the next fuzzer iteration, `parse_path_argument`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msees the stale [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon-NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pointer in `*arg`, and unconditionally frees it again via[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`free_and_replace`, triggering AddressSanitizer’s double-free detection.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Centralize ownership cleanup and pointer-reset semantics  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   To avoid ad-hoc checks in every function that frees buffers, we should [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrengthen the generic `freep` cleanup helper so that it not only frees the target [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer but also resets the caller’s pointer to `NULL`. This ensures that after any [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`_cleanup_free_` or `[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invocation, the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer is guaranteed to be `NULL`. Consequently, subsequent code that [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally frees the pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `parse_path_argument`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will safely call [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma no-op[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of freeing an already-freed address.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch `freep` in `src/basic/alloc-util.h`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Modify the inline definition of `freep` from:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     static inline void [0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid**[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     static inline void [0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         void **pp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid**[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m p;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*pp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         *pp = NULL;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This change preserves the existing signature and cleanup-macro machinery [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`_cleanup_free_`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but augments it to null pointers post-free.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other cleanup macros [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mfree`, `free_and_replace`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are altered.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `parse_path_argument` retains its semantics: it still frees the old argument [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon success, but since the pointer is now guaranteed to be `NULL` if already freed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the destructor, the free becomes a harmless `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All global pointers registered via `[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill likewise be nullified after cleanup, avoiding dangling pointers at program [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshutdown or in repeated fuzzer iterations.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and side-effect analysis  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This fix addresses the double-free by enforcing correct post-free state for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall cleanup functions that use `freep`.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves all existing command-line parsing and cleanup logic in systemd: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreep is only used in cleanup contexts [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatic-destruct, `_cleanup_free_`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msetting the pointer to NULL cannot break any code that runs post-shutdown.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only behavioral change is that after cleanup, global pointers become [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`NULL` rather than dangling—this is strictly safer and matches common cleanup [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatterns.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no modification to fuzz harness code, fuzzing logic, or external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries, ensuring compliance with project conventions and test-harness isolation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequirements.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Implementation steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `src/basic/alloc-util.h`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the `freep` function definition around line [0m[1;36m104[0m[39m.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Replace it with the null-assigning version shown above.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Rebuild and re-run the libFuzzer harness under AddressSanitizer to confirm [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe double-free is resolved.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Run the full test suite to ensure no regressions.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References in codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invokes destructors registered by [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvar, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` uses `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which calls [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `_cleanup_free_` macro expands to `[0m[1;35m_cleanup_[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfreep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, so all in-scope pointers[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musing it will now be nullified after free.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
